            <div class="text_contant_box">
             <span style="font-size: 26px; font-weight: bold; color: #11b4e4;">
              Welcome to Linear Recruitment.
             </span>
             <span style="color: #104c98; font-weight: bold;">
              We’re the People who make recruitment better.
             </span>
             <br/>
             To us, an outstanding construction recruitment agency means caring about the People you work with, and that’s why we’ve made it our business to place the right People in the right roles. We have expert teams of Construction Recruitment Consultants and Support Staff who are dedicated to providing a better brand of temporary, contract and permanent recruitment across a range of specialist industry sectors.

    jQuery(document).ready(function() {
 			//var container = document.querySelector('#masnory');
 			 jQuery('#masnory').masonry({
    			// options
     			itemSelector : '.item',
    			columnWidth :function( containerWidth ) {
     				return containerWidth / 35;
   				},
   			 });

   <script>
    jQuery(function() {
 			  	
 			          			
 			var availableTags = ["A17 Telescopic Handler - All Sizes ex. 360\u00b0 Slew","Assistant Site Manager","Bricklayers","Bricklaying Gang","CPCS","CPCS (Blue - Competant Operator)","CSCS (Blue - Craft)","CSCS (Green - Construction Site Operative)","CSCS Black","Civils","Engineer","Fabricator","Finishing","Finishing Foreman","First Aid","Floor Layer","Foreman","General Labourer","Graduate","Graduate Engineer","Groundwork","House Build","Housebuilding","Housing","Infrastructure","Labourer","Mechanical Fitter","Painter","Pipefitter","Plastic","Process Engineer","Quantity Surveying","Quantity Surveyor","SMSTS","SSSTS","Senior Quantity Surveyor","Site Manager","Skilled Labourer","Snagger","Technical Coordinator","Telehandler","Trades","Trades and labour","Waste Water","Water","Welder","construction","cscs","cscs labourer","engineering","plastic fabricator","plastic pipefitter","plastic welder","private housing"]   
 			 
 			    function split( val ) {
 			      return val.split( /,\s*/ );
 			    }
 			    function extractLast( term ) {
 			      return split( term ).pop();
 			    }
 			 
 			    jQuery( "#tag" )
 			      // don't navigate away from the field on tab when selecting an item
 			      .bind( "keydown", function( event ) {
 			        if ( event.keyCode === jQuery.ui.keyCode.TAB &&
 			            jQuery( this ).autocomplete( "instance" ).menu.active ) {
 			          event.preventDefault();
 			        }
 			      })
 			      .autocomplete({
 			        minLength: 0,
 			        source: function( request, response ) {
 			          // delegate back to autocomplete, but extract the last term
 			          response( jQuery.ui.autocomplete.filter(
 			            availableTags, extractLast( request.term ) ) );
 			        },
 			        focus: function() {
 			          // prevent value inserted on focus
 			          return false;
 			        },
 			        select: function( event, ui ) {
 			          var terms = split( this.value );
 			          // remove the current input
 			          terms.pop();
 			          // add the selected item
 			          terms.push( ui.item.value );
 			          // add placeholder to get the comma-and-space at the end
 			          terms.push( "" );
 			          this.value = terms.join( ", " );
 			          return false;
 			        }
 			      });
 			  });
   </script>

 			    jQuery( "#choosetag" )
 			      // don't navigate away from the field on tab when selecting an item
 			      .bind( "keydown", function( event ) {
 			        if ( event.keyCode === jQuery.ui.keyCode.TAB &&
 			            jQuery( this ).autocomplete( "instance" ).menu.active ) {
 			          event.preventDefault();
 			        }
 			      })
 			      .autocomplete({
 			        minLength: 0,
 			        source: function( request, response ) {
 			          // delegate back to autocomplete, but extract the last term
 			          response( jQuery.ui.autocomplete.filter(
 			            availableTags, extractLast( request.term ) ) );
 			        },
 			        focus: function() {
 			          // prevent value inserted on focus
 			          return false;
 			        },
 			        select: function( event, ui ) {
 			          var terms = split( this.value );
 			          // remove the current input
 			          terms.pop();
 			          // add the selected item
 			          terms.push( ui.item.value );
 			          // add placeholder to get the comma-and-space at the end
 			          terms.push( "" );
 			          this.value = terms.join( ", " );
 			          return false;
 			        }
 			      });
 			  });
   </script>

 						var availableTags = ["A17 Telescopic Handler - All Sizes ex. 360\u00b0 Slew","Assistant Site Manager","Bricklayers","Bricklaying Gang","CPCS","CPCS (Blue - Competant Operator)","CSCS (Blue - Craft)","CSCS (Green - Construction Site Operative)","CSCS Black","Civils","Engineer","Fabricator","Finishing","Finishing Foreman","First Aid","Floor Layer","Foreman","General Labourer","Graduate","Graduate Engineer","Groundwork","House Build","Housebuilding","Housing","Infrastructure","Labourer","Mechanical Fitter","Painter","Pipefitter","Plastic","Process Engineer","Quantity Surveying","Quantity Surveyor","SMSTS","SSSTS","Senior Quantity Surveyor","Site Manager","Skilled Labourer","Snagger","Technical Coordinator","Telehandler","Trades","Trades and labour","Waste Water","Water","Welder","construction","cscs","cscs labourer","engineering","plastic fabricator","plastic pipefitter","plastic welder","private housing"]   
 			 
 			    function split( val ) {
 			      return val.split( /,\s*/ );
 			    }
 			    function extractLast( term ) {
 			      return split( term ).pop();
 			    }
 			 
 			    jQuery( "#industrial-engineering" )
 			      // don't navigate away from the field on tab when selecting an item
 			      .bind( "keydown", function( event ) {
 			        if ( event.keyCode === jQuery.ui.keyCode.TAB &&
 			            jQuery( this ).autocomplete( "instance" ).menu.active ) {
 			          event.preventDefault();
 			        }
 			      })
 			      .autocomplete({
 			        minLength: 0,
 			        source: function( request, response ) {
 			          // delegate back to autocomplete, but extract the last term
 			          response( jQuery.ui.autocomplete.filter(
 			            availableTags, extractLast( request.term ) ) );
 			        },
 			        focus: function() {
 			          // prevent value inserted on focus
 			          return false;
 			        },
 			        select: function( event, ui ) {
 			          var terms = split( this.value );
 			          // remove the current input
 			          terms.pop();
 			          // add the selected item
 			          terms.push( ui.item.value );
 			          // add placeholder to get the comma-and-space at the end
 			          terms.push( "" );
 			          this.value = terms.join( ", " );
 			          return false;
 			        }
 			      });
 			  });
   </script>
   <script>
    function checkKeywords()
 	{
 		var keys=document.getElementById('tags').value;
 		if(keys== '')
 		{
 			alert('Please Enter Search Keywords.');
 			return false;
 		}
 	 return true;
 	}
   </script>

 					jQuery(".active i").removeClass("fa fa-minus");
 				 	jQuery(".active i").addClass("fa fa-plus");				 	
 				 	jQuery(this).parent().find('a').removeClass('active');
 		 	
 				 }
 			 });
 			 var placeholder;
 			 var placeholder_val;
 			 jQuery('input,textarea').focusin(function(){
    				placeholder = jQuery(this).attr("placeholder");
    				if(placeholder!= "" || placeholder!= null || placeholder!= "undefined"){
    					placeholder_val=placeholder;
    				}
    				//alert(placeholder);
    				jQuery(this).removeAttr('placeholder');
 			 });
 			 jQuery('input,textarea').focusout(function(){
 			 	//alert(placeholder_val);
    				jQuery(this).attr('placeholder', placeholder_val);
    				
 			 });
 		});

   <script type="text/javascript">
    function showPostDescription(postlink,post)
 	 	  	{
 	 	  		if(jQuery(post).css('display') == 'none')
 	 	  		{
 		 	  		jQuery(post).slideDown("3000");
 		 	  		jQuery(postlink).toggleClass("fa-plus fa-minus");
 	 	  		}
 	 	  		else
 	 	  		{
 	 	  			jQuery(post).slideUp("3000");
 		 	  		jQuery(postlink).toggleClass("fa-minus fa-plus");
 	 	  		}
 	 	  	}
   </script>
